# Deviation Report: M2 Model Structure

This report shows deviations between the documented AUTOSAR M2 model structure
and the actual Python implementation.

## Summary

- ✓ **Match**: 155 classes correctly implemented
- ✗ **Missing**: 1189 classes documented but not found
- ⚠ **Path Mismatch**: 542 classes in wrong location
- + **Extra**: 207 undocumented classes
- **Total Documented Classes**: 1886
- **Total Deviations**: 1938
